[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction htmlSecureComment [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:3591[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, triggered by a call to [0m             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation. The issue was uncovered by a libFuzzer-based harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzz/html.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring an interactive fuzzing session.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - A multi-byte write of [0m[1;36m105[0m[39m bytes overruns a heap buffer by exactly [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes past [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mits [0m[1;36m501[0m[39m-byte allocation.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The overflow is detected at address [0m[1;36m0x515000000775[0m[39m, immediately beyond the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated region [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x515000000580[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x515000000775[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations and findings:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The failing instruction is `__asan_memcpy` invoked within `htmlSecureComment` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min HTMLparser.c at line [0m[1;36m3591[0m[39m.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhtmlCtxtParseDocument → LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput → libFuzzer’s FuzzerLoop.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The buffer in question is allocated by `xmlFuzzMalloc` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzz/fuzz.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcauses a write just past the end of that region.[0m                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling logic in the comment parser may miscompute buffer boundaries.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify and isolate the faulty reallocation logic in htmlSecureComment:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Open HTMLparser.c and locate the function htmlSecureComment.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Within the main copy-and-grow loop, find the block beginning at the existing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguard:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Correct the growth condition:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the guard `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     so that the decision to reallocate accounts for both the data already in the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`used`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the incoming chunk [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`extraSize`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Synchronize the capacity variable:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inside the same reallocation block, after successfully calling xmlRealloc:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        – Assign the returned pointer to `buffer`.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        – Update the local `buffer_size` to the newly allocated capacity [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`newSize`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ensuring subsequent iterations see the correct buffer capacity.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Mirror the proven logic in htmlParseData:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify that your patched logic now matches the pattern used in htmlParseData’s[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresizing:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            size_t newSize = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            tmp = [0m[1;35mxmlRealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, newSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            … buffer = tmp;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            buffer_size = newSize;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Preserve existing functionality and error handling:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain the doubling growth strategy and the `+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` for NUL-termination.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep the `[0m[1;35mhtmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `goto error` on realloc failure.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not alter any logic outside this specific buffer-resize guard.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Add a regression test:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Create or extend a minimal HTML comment fuzz testcase that previously [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered the overflow.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that after patching, the [0m[1;36m501[0m[39m-byte allocation cannot be overrun, and no[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer errors occur when writing up to the doubled size.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Run full regression suite:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure no other HTML parsing tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding those for comments, entities, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscripts, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m regress.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify that all existing libxml2 unit tests and fuzz harnesses still pass.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The root cause was an off-by-logic in the growth check: only the incoming chunk [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize was compared against the current capacity, ignoring previously written data. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBy switching to `used + extraSize`, we guarantee the buffer is enlarged whenever [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe total data cannot fit.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Updating `buffer_size` after realloc aligns with how htmlParseData manages its [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocal capacity, preserving the doubling strategy and maintaining NUL-space for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtermination.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This approach does not alter external APIs, fuzz harnesses, or test code, and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoids any broad or silent exception catching. It directly fixes the miscalculation[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat its source while preserving all other behavior.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch attempt[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The condition `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` was replaced with `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Inside that branch, the code doubles the buffer size and calls `xmlRealloc`.  [0m [2m                [0m
